Current Events Commentary

The Current Crisis in European Politics 16

— Ming

(1)

The strained relationship between France and Germany, inherited from history, cannot be easily resolved in the short term. Moreover, France is vigilantly prepared, fearing that once Germany's military strength is restored, Paris will again be besieged. Therefore, it insists on "security guarantees," believing that if France's security is firmly assured, other issues will be easily resolved. On the German side, dissatisfied with the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles and deeply feeling the pressure of economic panic, it realizes that this economic panic cannot be broken in an instant, and it is not easy to find a way out through the economy itself. Only by opening a path politically can economic solutions be sought. Hitler took the destruction of unequal treaties as his rallying cry to enter the political stage. Therefore, he must resolutely insist that Germany cannot be left defenseless against its neighbors' guns. The demand for "equality in armaments" does have its grand justification.

Since Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations, the European situation has suddenly become tense. Because Germany's withdrawal will inevitably lead to its unilateral abandonment of the Treaty of Versailles to expand its military strength according to its own wishes. At this time, France would never stand idly by and would surely take up arms. At the same time, the small countries that are France's satellites would follow in France's footsteps and actively engage in military preparations. However, in this crisis-ridden and explosive situation, Britain's actions are crucial. Britain's traditional policy towards Europe is to prevent any single country from dominating the continent. Before the war, Germany was too strong, and Britain would take the opportunity to strike it down. How is Britain's attitude towards France any different now? Although Britain's pro-French inclination has not changed, the opinions of Britain and France differ greatly on relations with Germany, especially regarding arms reduction. Britain believes that after the end of the "trial period," if France cannot prove that Germany has violated the agreement during this period, then France has an obligation to immediately reduce its armaments. However, France insists that Germany must show sincerity in seeking peace and demonstrate that it has no intention of violating the arms reduction agreement before France can reduce its armaments. Even if Britain's view could be realized, Germany might not agree. Moreover, France still has this argument. Italy fundamentally rejects Germany's demand for equality in armaments.

Furthermore, the Fascist leader Italy, in theory and in practice, has not proven to be truly aligned with Germany to the end. However, currently, Italy is eager to develop its colonies in North Africa and needs hegemony in the Mediterranean. It wants to be the leader of the small countries in Central Europe, and of course, Italy wants to exclusively control the Adriatic Sea. Therefore, Italy also expresses dissatisfaction with the Treaty of Versailles, thus indirectly sympathizing with Germany. The opposition between Italy and France is becoming increasingly acute, both at sea and on land. (2)

On the other hand, there is the Soviet Union, which was formerly watched by all capitalist countries and is still regarded as important, and now has even greater influence. Previously, German diplomacy cleverly used its relations with the Soviet Union to restrain Britain and France. Therefore, even in a situation of surrounding pressure, it was still able to open up a political path for itself. Unexpectedly, after Hitler came to power, driven by momentary emotional impulses, he made relations with the Soviet Union extremely bad.

At this time, France realized that the Soviet Union had the potential to influence the European political situation, and that France's intention to defend against Germany would naturally outweigh its defense against the Soviet Union. Therefore, taking this opportunity, it signed a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union. In early September 1933, former Premier Herriot, accompanied by representatives of the French government, went to Moscow and was warmly welcomed by the Soviet authorities. In mid-September, the French Minister of Aviation led three aircraft to visit Moscow from the air. Such actions by the current minister were unprecedented in the Soviet Union's foreign relations. This proves that the friendly relationship between France and the Soviet Union is becoming increasingly close.

We can see the change in French foreign policy from Herriot's theory of French-Russian friendship. Since France intends to get closer to the Soviet Union, the small countries of Central Europe will naturally follow France's lead and engage in friendly relations with France. On the surface, this seems to be a symbol of the peace movement, but in reality, it is the eve of armed conflict. When arms preparation has reached its peak, such diplomatic maneuvering, at least, is to pay full attention to the development of the war crisis and is an extremely serious preparation for war!

(3)

The crisis is constantly developing there and is still adding new elements. We cannot but try to examine the place where the crisis erupted and the core where the crisis is latent. Everyone knows from history that before the World War, the Balkans were the powder keg of Europe. As a result, a bullet in Sarajevo triggered World War I. Now the situation has changed, and Europe has more than one powder keg.

Among those powder kegs, the issue of the corridor between Germany and Poland is the easiest to explode and the most dangerous. The so-called German-Polish corridor, on the Polish side, certainly provided an outlet to the sea, and Poland was no longer restricted by German imperialism. However, on the German side, the territory of East Prussia was forcibly separated. This is unbearable not only for the Prussian "Junkers" (noble landowners), but also for the general German population who harbor resentment. Moreover, German nationalism is highly developed, so the call to overthrow the Treaty of Versailles permeates all of Germany. This is the most urgent crisis in the European political situation.

Secondly, the relationship between the two Central European countries, Austria and Hungary, and the small Entente countries in the Danube region is entangled with ethnic issues, general political relations, and economic relations. France uses this to forge its hegemony in Europe, and Italy also wants to play a role at this time, so the problem becomes even more serious. At the same time, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania will never allow Germany's power to expand excessively. Although their existing strength is not enough to prevent the German-Austrian union movement, they can ask for France's help and Italy's cooperation, which is exactly what the two countries are about to do. Therefore, the disputes in Central Europe have added another explosive element. From the above brief description, we can see the complexity of the disputes and the seriousness of the crisis in the opposition between European countries.

President Wang's Thoughts on the Fujian Incident 19

— Speech at the Central Memorial Week

Private Armies Should Be Eliminated

(Nanjing) The Central Committee held the 112th Memorial Week at 9:00 am on the 8th. Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Zhang Ji, Wang Zhaoming, Chen Lifu, Li Zonghuang, Zheng Zhan'an, Xie Zuofa, Wang Qi, Zeng Zhongming, Ji Liang, and staff members, totaling more than 600 people, attended. Wang Zhaoming presided over the meeting and made the following report:

Comrades, what I want to say today is just a very simple point, that is, about the rebellion of Chen and Li in Fujian and the feelings that have arisen from it. Since the September 18th Incident, comrades of our party have felt the seriousness of the national crisis, put aside all previous disputes, and advocated unity to jointly shoulder the responsibility of saving the nation and preserving its existence. In the past two years, although there are still various regrets about the effect of unity, the terrible civil war has finally been avoided. Although local conflicts still occur from time to time, the central government has always maintained an attitude of appeasement towards the localities and is unwilling to break ties lightly, because saving the nation and preserving its existence is more important than internal unity. In these two years, the use of force domestically has been limited to suppressing the communists, because the communists do not want the motherland and cannot be talked to about saving the nation and preserving its existence. When the Battle of Shanghai was urgent the year before last, the central government transferred troops from Jiangxi to support, but they took the opportunity to attack Ganzhou. When the war in North China was urgent last year, the central government transferred troops from Jiangxi to support, but they took the opportunity to attack Nanchang. From these two incidents, everyone knows that if we do not do our best to suppress the communists, then the work of saving the nation and preserving its existence cannot be started. Recently, Chen and Li rebelled in Fujian. Their goal is to overthrow the Republic of China and abandon the Chinese Kuomintang. Their desire to abandon the motherland is the same as the communists, so they resolutely allied with the communists. In fact, it cannot be said that they allied with the communists, it can only be said that they surrendered to the communists. The central government had no choice but to adopt the method of suppressing the communists to suppress them. At this time, some people advocated peaceful solutions, and some advocated a ceasefire. Their method of peaceful resolution was to have Chen and Li abolish the puppet state and puppet government, and at the same time have the central government reform the political system and what they called "the path of virtue should not be avoided." We can imagine whether this kind of advocacy is possible to realize. Are Chen and Li dissatisfied with the political system or with the people? If so, why did they have to abolish the Republic of China and abolish the Chinese Kuomintang? Therefore, the method of peaceful resolution will not have any effect on Chen and Li's side, but it will cause great danger on the central government's side, because today, Chen and Li's side wants to abandon the party and the country, and the central government's side wants to maintain the party and the country. In this struggle, if various reform plans are suddenly proposed, it is tantamount to causing internal turmoil in the central government, tantamount to responding to Chen and Li in order to carry out the plan to subvert the central government. If the central government is unfortunately overthrown, then the work of maintaining the party and the country will be eliminated along with it. This is such a great danger, so the four words "peaceful resolution" contain countless conspiracies and evils. All my comrades must deeply recognize this. In short, Chen and Li's rebellion cannot coexist with the party and the country. There is really no other way to save it except to do our best to suppress it. This is a palliative work. If all my comrades remember that we are saving the nation and preserving its existence and not suppressing Chen and Li who rebelled and surrendered to the communists, then of course they will not have any objections. What I want to say now is that in addition to these palliative works, we should further discuss a more fundamental problem. This problem is how did the 19th Route Army rebel? How did Chen and Li make the 19th Route Army rebel? In the 14th year, the 19th Route Army was a part of the National Revolutionary Army. In the 15th year, it was a part of the Northern Expeditionary Army. Since then, it has done a lot of work in suppressing bandits and resisting Japan. It was transferred to Fujian the year before last, and its only task was to suppress the communists. It was entrusted with the task of the East Route, hoping that it could cooperate with the North Route, West Route, and South Route to complete the plan of encirclement and annihilation. Its efforts have been like this, and its current task is also like this. Why does an army of the National Revolution openly do things that betray the National Revolution? Why does an army that suppresses communists openly do things that ally with the communists or even surrender to the communists? If it is said that it is due to the instigation of Chen and Li's ambitions, then why do all the officers and soldiers of the 19th Route Army blindly and blindly listen to his instructions? According to this, if Chen and Li were to become emperors one day, all the officers and soldiers of the 19th Route Army would stage the story of Chenqiao welcoming the Emperor in Yellow Robes. This phenomenon is very surprising, and what is the cause of this phenomenon? This is what we must carefully examine. Naturally, China has a vast territory, inconvenient transportation, and political and economic forces are not easy to concentrate, so military rebellion can occur at any time. However, the military organization is not perfect and the military training is not fully implemented, so the quality of the soldiers is poor and they are easily manipulated by the officers. As long as there are ambitious and ambitious officers, they can organize a cadre to drive the soldiers and make them become a private system. Today, they are soldiers of the National Revolutionary Army, flying the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun, and tomorrow they are communist dogs, flying the flag of the Red Land with a Yellow Star. They can do anything. If this phenomenon and this cause cannot be eradicated, then the future of the Republic of China will have endless obstacles. Regarding this point, I think our comrades must have a clear understanding. If we do not pay attention to this and go to discuss what political system, I think it is ineffective. For example, recently some people have advocated opening up political power, and their purpose is to end political tutelage and start constitutionalism in advance. Some people advocate maintaining the party's dictatorship. In fact, these disputes were decided by the Prime Minister before his death. The Prime Minister advocated that political tutelage is an indispensable stage in the process of national revolution, because the national revolution must eliminate everything and build everything. Without political tutelage, it is impossible to concentrate political and economic forces. At the same time, the Prime Minister also explained the purpose of political tutelage and pointed out the difference between political tutelage and enlightened autocracy. The Prime Minister said that enlightened autocracy takes autocracy as its purpose, while political tutelage takes republicanism as its purpose. Therefore, vigorously implementing party rule and cultivating civil rights is the only way out for the national revolution, and there is no need to come and argue again. Now I won't go into details, but what I want to earnestly explain is that if private armies cannot be fundamentally eliminated, then constitutionalism cannot be realized, and even political tutelage cannot be realized. The existence of private armies is rampant and unscrupulous, then the so-called constitutionalism cannot be implemented, which is unnecessary to say. Why do I say that even political tutelage cannot be realized? Now some people feel the chaos of national affairs and think that if we can have a fascist dictatorship like Italy, it is not a way to revitalize and remedy the ills. But let us think about how many troops Italy sent before the fascist dictatorship, when it participated in the war? The total number exceeded four million. How many people died or were injured? More than 650,000 died, more than 450,000 were disabled, and more than 1 million were injured. And when the Fascist Party marched on Rome, the number of the so-called four legions, according to the opposition party, was only more than 10,000. Even according to Mussolini's autobiography, the number of Blackshirts who were armed after the successful march on Rome was only more than 60,000. And when the march on Rome, the government issued an order for the army to suppress it, but the army refused to obey, so the government collapsed, and Mussolini was ordered to form a cabinet to implement the policies of the Fascist Party. From this, we can see that before the Fascist Party's dictatorship in Italy, its army was used for foreign wars and not for internal wars. The change of regime in its country was based on the expression of public opinion, not on the victory or defeat of the army. Before the Fascist Party marched on Rome, the Communist Party occupied factories everywhere, destroyed traffic, and caused unbearable harassment, completely losing the sympathy of the people. The government was weak and incompetent, and hesitant, completely losing the faith of the people. Therefore, the army did not hinder the Fascist Party's march on Rome because the army had some common sense, so Mussolini could rely on it to implement his policies. If the Italian army at that time was like a private army, then some of them would have helped the government to attack the Fascist Party marching on Rome, and some of them would have helped the Fascist Party to attack the government. In this way, Italy would have been split and fought a big fight without end. How could there have been such an easy march on Rome? From this, we can know that if private armies are not fundamentally eliminated, not only will constitutionalism not be realized, but even political tutelage will not be realized. This is by no means an overstatement. For several years, some people have said that political tutelage has not achieved results. In fact, it is not that political tutelage has not achieved results, but that political tutelage has not started. The reason why political tutelage cannot start is because the above-mentioned obstacles have not been removed. This is what we are very sad about, and we cannot but admit it. If we see this clearly, then in addition to the so-called palliative work, we should work harder on the fundamental work. The so-called fundamental work is to improve military organization, strengthen military training, break the private system, and cultivate a pure and consistent National Revolutionary Army, which is certainly necessary. But what is even more necessary is to cultivate civil rights. The so-called cultivation of civil rights is not only to increase the political power of the people, but also to increase the economic power of the people. According to the national organization of modern people and its relationship in the world, the survival of the nation and the nation lies in economic self-sufficiency. The so-called political power is only used as a guarantee for economic power and to eliminate its obstacles. Therefore, the so-called civil rights should also focus on economic development. With economic development, the power of the people will naturally increase. Not only can they judge private armies, but also make private armies fundamentally unable to occur and exist. This can be said to be the fundamental work in the fundamental work. We must know that guns can certainly punish reaction, but they can also fundamentally eliminate reaction. I said before that there is no more urgent task than production and construction, and its meaning lies in this. Last November and December, our comrades suffered countless pains and oppressions in their hearts because of Chen and Li's rebellion in Fujian. From this pain and oppression, we have generated a kind of courage. We are doubly sincere and united, doubly clear about the doctrine, and doubly striving to implement it. In this way, we will be able to lay the foundation of the national revolution in this turbulent environment. (Special Telegram, 8th)

Kong Xiangxi Reports on Key Economic Relief Strategies 20

｜At the National Government Memorial Week｜

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangxi reported on the morning of the 8th, during the National Government Memorial Week, on the key strategies to alleviate China's economic crisis. He stated that recently, various countries are plagued by economic downturns, and our country, due to its underdeveloped industries, is less affected. However, with the depreciation of gold and appreciation of silver, our country, which has always had a trade deficit, will inevitably face increasing population and declining exports. Our country has traditionally relied on three factors to offset the trade deficit: firstly, remittances from overseas Chinese; secondly, investments by foreigners in business and industry in China; and thirdly, funding for missionary and charitable relief efforts by foreigners in China. Now that various countries are experiencing economic downturns, these capital inflows will inevitably decrease, and the economic downturn will gradually affect our country. We should prepare in advance to prevent disaster. Today, I would like to offer for your reference my personal research on China's economic problems, so as to achieve better methods and avoid social dangers. Currently, the largest source of central government revenue is customs duties, amounting to over thirty million yuan annually. However, due to the Boxer Indemnity, customs duties have been used annually to repay the debt since the 27th year of Emperor Guangxu's reign, and it will take another fourteen years to fully repay. Therefore, most of the customs duties are used to repay the indemnity. After the establishment of the National Government, the great powers expressed goodwill and returned the Boxer Indemnity, but most of it was designated as funds for cultural and educational construction, and the government cannot arbitrarily use it. In addition, some are designated as collateral for public bonds. Apart from these, the monthly surplus is only about five million. The second largest source of revenue is the salt tax, amounting to about one hundred forty to fifty million annually. However, tax rates vary across regions, ranging from one to thirteen yuan per dan (unit of weight). It is proposed to uniformly reduce tax rates above ten yuan to ten yuan to equalize the burden. After deducting debt repayments, the government receives only five million per month from the salt tax. Thirdly, is the consolidated tax. Since the implementation of the consolidated tax in the twentieth year, the largest sources of revenue have been from cigarettes and cotton yarn. Most yarn factories are operated by Japanese interests, with strong capital and advanced technology, coupled with the full assistance of their government, they are dumping products in China. In a few years, whether Chinese yarn factories can survive is highly questionable. Other industries such as cement and matches also face similar dangers. Currently, the monthly consolidated tax revenue is seven million yuan. The above three sources total seventeen million, plus another two to three million from various other taxes, the total monthly revenue is only eighteen to nineteen million. On the expenditure side, military and government construction require thirty-five million per month, resulting in a monthly deficit of about fifteen million, and an annual loss of one hundred seventy to eighty million. With such income and expenditure, at a time when the people are suffering greatly, even if we exhaust all resources, the gains will be minimal. For example, last year, we increased import duties on white sugar because it is a luxury item, but as a result, due to smuggling by unscrupulous merchants, the revenue was only 48% of what it was before. To prevent smuggling, a strict organization is required, but the country lacks the funds to establish such a customs enforcement force, so tax revenues are affected. Currently, financial difficulties are not limited to China; even in powerful countries, the amount of the deficit is alarming. The US President has proposed to increase the issuance of ten billion (US dollars) of US public bonds. If it were in our country, even one-tenth of that amount would be impossible to achieve. To make the country wealthy and the people strong, there must be a solution to the financial problems, and the people must be made prosperous. Currently, Chinese society faces immense difficulties. If we do not strive for relief, the economic downturn will spread within a year. Previously, gold was expensive and silver was cheap, and Chinese goods were cheap due to the use of silver, so we could compete in the world market. Because gold was expensive, foreign goods were expensive, and we could buy fewer unnecessary goods, resulting in less outflow of money. But with gold cheap and silver expensive, our exports will inevitably decrease, and imports will increase, resulting in a growing trade deficit each year. The social economy will truly be unimaginable. The Chinese economic situation is declining so rapidly that the way to provide relief must be to pay attention to economics, "Economic" relief to China's future crisis, tracing back to the source, we should promote thrift. In the past, life was very frugal. We hired scholars to educate our children, and the annual cost was only one hundred and twenty taels of silver. But now, educating children costs both the family and the government a great deal. However, the standard of living continues to rise. If the government does not seek relief, the people's lives will become unsustainable. Therefore, I propose the word "thrift" and ask everyone to practice it. The government should especially take the lead to set an example. The government's steps for thrift are: first, save on recurrent expenses; second, increase business expenses; and third, have rational construction. In recent years, people in our country have talked about construction, but construction without a plan is the same as no construction. For example, in recent years, the United States has experienced over-construction, overproduction, and uneven distribution, so the people's purchasing power has not increased, leading to economic panic. Other examples include coffee in Central and South America and sugar in Cuba, which are all overproduced and thrown into the sea. Now, when we talk about construction, if we do not have an overall plan and act rashly, the government will definitely suffer more than it benefits. Fourth, promote people's savings. France is a debtor nation, but the French have a habit of saving, and banks have a lot of deposits. People in our country not only do not have a habit of saving, but those with an income of one hundred yuan spend one hundred and twenty yuan, spending all their income and even falling into debt. Another group of people, although not wasteful, like to bury their money underground, hindering economic activity. Therefore, the government should promote savings and provide reliable guarantees. In addition, there is one more point, which is to promote dietary restraint. Foreigners have moderation in their diet, but in Chinese homes, tables are filled with dishes, especially in cities, where it is even more extravagant, spending dozens of dollars on a meal without hesitation. It is not an exaggeration to say that people eat themselves into poverty. We should quickly publicize the need to eliminate gluttony, and other forms of waste should also be prevented. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings require us to build the nation, and we should save and build at the same time, and it should be planned construction. In the past, Chinese politics followed Confucius's idea of ​​using the people at the right time, using the slack season in winter to carry out construction projects. Now, if we want to make the party and the country stable and strong, the first thing to do is to carry out rational construction from an economic perspective. China is an agricultural country, and we must start by helping farmers, building rural areas, and increasing production. Chinese farmers bear too heavy a burden. When I was Minister of Industry and Commerce, I strongly advocated abolishing the likin (internal transit tax), but after the abolition of the likin, local authorities increased additional taxes, so that the burden on farmers became heavier. Not only are they doomed to die in bad years, but even in good years, they cannot live in peace due to heavy taxes. Now, if we want to increase production, we must have a comprehensive plan to promote benefits and eliminate disadvantages. We must not only guard against deficiencies but also guard against surpluses, so that supply and demand correspond and are moderate. This will ensure that the economic downturn does not affect China. (Central News Agency, 8th)

Kong Xiangxi Returns to Nanjing with Financial Solutions 21

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangxi went to Shanghai at the end of the year to celebrate the New Year and discussed important financial matters with various sectors in Shanghai. He returned to Nanjing on the morning of the 8th and went to his ministry. It is reported that the central government's finances are very stable. The expenses for party, government, and military affairs in January, as well as the military expenses for suppressing the rebellion in Fujian, have all been arranged. Currently, efforts are being made to find new sources of revenue without increasing the burden on the people. It is expected that the central government's financial revenue and expenditure will be balanced in about six months. As for the Shanghai newspaper reports that Finance Minister Kong has borrowed another one million yuan from the Shanghai financial industry, this is actually the remaining amount of the previously agreed two million yuan loan. Only one million was delivered at that time, and the remaining amount was only recently paid in full, leading to the misunderstanding that a new loan was borrowed. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Ministry of Industry's Fishery Market Plan 22

Commercial Shares Account for One-Third

The capital is tentatively set at 1.5 million yuan, with government shares accounting for two-thirds and commercial shares accounting for one-third. The fishery market will be located in Shanghai, on the newly filled beach area of ​​Yangshupu and Dingpu Bureau, along the shore. The entire site will be constructed, divided into (1) retail and auction market, (2) market office, (3) broker auction market, (4) broker market, (5) salted goods wharf, (6) seagoing ship wharf. Regarding the construction of the cold storage, it will include (1) cold storage room, (2) freezing room, (3) production room, (4) ice storage room, (5) cold storage office, (6) machine room. In addition, a financial room and a wireless weather station will also be built. It is hoped that there will be no major financial problems, and construction will begin soon. (Special dispatch, 8th)

American and Russian Ambassadors Arrive in Washington on the Same Ship 29

Russian Ambassador Declares Willingness to Work for Peace

Avoids Answering Questions About Japanese-Russian Relations

(Washington) The first Soviet Russian Ambassador to the United States, Troyanovsky, and the first American Ambassador to Russia, Bullitt, arrived here at the same time. Bullitt recently went to Russia to present his credentials and then returned to the United States to discuss the establishment of the embassy with President Roosevelt and report on his initial impressions of the Soviet Union. He crossed the Atlantic with Troyanovsky on the same ship. When the two arrived here, many senior officials from the State Department came to the station to welcome them. Troyanovsky gave a speech by radio, saying that he was willing to "work for world peace." Troyanovsky then told reporters that the rapprochement between the United States and Russia at a time when various Far Eastern problems are unresolved is "It may be that in the future some situation will occur that will make people feel that the US-Russian rapprochement is a good thing. What the future holds will depend on future circumstances and needs." Troyanovsky added that it is not known whether such a need will ever arise. Troyanovsky avoided answering questions about Japanese-Russian relations, but said, "In reality, world history will become the history of the Pacific Ocean. We are now entering this history, but the Atlantic era has not yet ended. Major events are developing in the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans, and the United States and Russia are concerned about all events along the coasts of the two oceans and the seas surrounding them. American Ambassador to Russia Bullitt declared that he is scheduled to return to Moscow around February 1 to take office. (Havas, 7th)

Roosevelt Plans to Ask Congress for Special Power to Negotiate Tax Treaties 33

Protection Tax Plan Delayed

Abandoning the Strong Policy on War Debts

Willing to Automatically Reduce Finland's by 50%

(Washington) The "Commercial News", known for its well-informed sources, reported that President Roosevelt decided last night to wait for a more favorable opportunity to request broad powers from Congress to engage in negotiations on trade agreements and tariff treaties. The reason is the increasing number of protests from the industrial sector against Roosevelt's commercial advisor's plans. Therefore, Roosevelt had to postpone requesting broad powers from Congress. The plan drafted by the Senate Tariff Committee will also be delayed in its release. The main purpose of the plan is to protect various industries with potential for development. Other industries, although protected by tariffs, still have insufficient domestic consumption in the United States, or the national demand is very limited. Even if tariff protection is added, they still have no extraordinary development capabilities. Certain goods, such as rayon, are hardly affected by foreign competition. The import of American rayon is only one percent of domestic production. The tariffs on these goods can be further reduced to stimulate American production. Furthermore, taxes cannot be increased on manganese imported from Russia, because American manganese products are more labor-intensive than those from Russia, and the U.S. Navy Department must store domestically produced manganese to meet wartime needs. Therefore, there is no need to increase the import tax on manganese. (Havas, 8th)

(Washington) According to the "New York Public Forum", President Roosevelt requested Congress to revise Finland's war debt to the United States in a spirit of special friendship, reducing the total amount of war debt by 50%. Finland is the only country that has fully repaid its war debt on time. The President's move is the first break from the U.S. government's hard-line policy on war debts. At the same time, it is a warning and hint to countries that have defaulted or only paid a portion of their war debts on time, and indicates the limit of concessions on war debts. Because Finland has not defaulted on war debt payments, and is only able to obtain a 50% reduction, then when other countries reopen war debt negotiations with the United States, the United States' concession will also not exceed this 50% limit. (Havas, 8th)

Special Tax Measures for Fujian Province's Native Tobacco 43

(Nanjing) The special tax on native tobacco leaves in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian was originally listed as a special tax zone. Currently, the political upheaval in Fujian province has not yet complied. All native tobacco leaves and their manufactured tobacco shreds in the province transported into the other six special tax provinces, as instructed by the Ministry of Finance, are to be handled according to the methods for non-special tax zones. The first responsible special tax agency at the point of entry will uniformly collect the special tax, issue a tax-paid certificate valid in the special tax zone, and affix an imprinted photo to the package before allowing transportation. Those requiring customs clearance should also fill out a yellow declaration form, along with the tax-paid certificate and other documents, and send them to customs for verification before allowing import. Those who have paid the special tax on native tobacco leaves and tobacco shreds in the six special tax zone provinces and transport them to Fujian province should temporarily handle them uniformly according to the regulations for transporting to non-special tax zones. Merchants are allowed to present the original tax certificate, or sub-transport certificate with other supporting documents, along with the tax collection evidence for transportation to the province, to the responsible special tax agency for verification and return of half of the original special tax paid, that is, a refund of two yuan and three cents and five li per hundred market catties, to show compassion. Yesterday, the Customs Administration and the provincial stamp and alcohol tax bureaus were ordered to comply. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Hangzhou) It began to snow heavily in Hangzhou for the first time on the evening of the 7th after 2:00 AM. On the morning of the 8th, there was an inch of snow accumulation in the inland area, and there was still an intention for continued snowfall. (Central News Agency, 8th)

A Record of Wu Chaoshu's Passing 65

=From the Onset of Illness to Sudden Death in Just a Few Hours=

=Funeral Held on the 4th, Cremated at the Indian Cemetery=

Hong Kong Correspondence: Wu Chaoshu, a member of the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang, suddenly suffered a stroke due to cerebral anemia at 1:00 PM on the 2nd of this month and passed away at his private residence on Hing Han Road, Hong Kong. The coffin was closed at noon on the 3rd, and the funeral was held at 2:00 PM on the 4th, with cremation at the Indian Cemetery in Happy Valley. Over a thousand prominent figures and gentry and merchants from Hong Kong and China attended the funeral. Many condolence messages were also sent from the central and Guangdong-Guangxi authorities. The details are recorded as follows:

Wu returned to Hong Kong from Shanghai several months ago and resided in his private residence in Kai Tak, Kowloon, and he refrained from politics, spending his days reading and rarely going out. Recently, he moved to the third floor of No. 3 Hing Han Road, Sai Ying Pun. The building was originally inhabited by his children to facilitate their studies at various schools in Hong Kong and China. Wu was physically strong and rarely sick, but at 10:30 AM on the 2nd of this month, he suddenly had a severe headache and asked his family to get aspirin for him. His family obeyed, but it was ineffective. By 11:00 AM, the pain had intensified, and he soon fainted and lost consciousness. His wife urgently summoned Dr. Chile Lao, head of the Medical Department of the University of Hong Kong, Guo Shengde, and his son-in-law, Dr. Ma Huimin, for consultation. At that time, the doctors diagnosed cerebral anemia and rupture of a major blood vessel and were planning to perform a blood transfusion, injecting fresh blood from others, but before they could take action, Wu passed away at 1:30 PM.

Wu's passing was deeply mourned by his wife, children, relatives, and friends in Hong Kong and China. A funeral arrangement office was set up at the residence, and reports were sent to friends and relatives in all directions. His body was closed in a coffin at noon on the 3rd. At the time of the closure, Wu's wife, his three sons and five daughters, were on the verge of collapse from grief, and were still wailing despite the comfort of relatives and friends. Hu Hanmin and Sun Ke personally came to pay their respects, and Hu could not help but shed old tears upon seeing the scene. The Southwest Political Affairs Council sent Luo Yiqun to Hong Kong to represent the memorial service. The others present were Gan Jiahai, Foreign Affairs Inspector of the Five Provinces, Hu Hanmin's daughter Mulan, Deng Zhaoyin, Zou Dianbang, Luo Xuefu, Hong Kong gentry Cao Shanyun, Ma Yongcan, and others, totaling several hundred people.

The funeral was held at 2:00 PM on the 4th. The ceremony was very simple, and cremation was used for the funeral. One hour before the funeral, Chinese and foreign relatives and friends continued to gather at Wu's residence, blocking Hing Han Road. At the sound of the bell, the mourners bowed three times to the coffin in order to pay their respects. After the tribute, the hearse set off, adorned with fresh flowers, which was quite magnificent. Wu's wife, his three sons and five daughters, all dressed in mourning clothes and straw sandals, followed along crying, extremely saddened. The hearse then passed from Hing Han Road to Bonham Road to Caine Road, out of Garden Road to Lower Albert Road, through the East Main Street, and to the Indian Cemetery at Happy Valley. Their order of procession was as follows: (1) The banner with the words "Wu Family Funeral" adorned with fresh flowers, (2) Wu's portrait, (3) Hundreds of wreaths from the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and prominent figures such as Lin Sen, Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, He Yingqin, Kong Xiangxi, Song Ziwen, Zhu Peide, Chen Zhaoying, Zhang Ji, Chen Jitang, Li Jishen, and Wu Tiecheng, (4) Students from St. Paul's School, male and female students from Minsheng College, students from Wanchai School, and students from Ying Wah College, (5) Mourning garments, (6) Hearse, (7) Relatives and friends in attendance. The procession, with plain cars and white horses, stretched for hundreds of feet, and the number of onlookers along the way was countless.

At 4:00 PM, the hearse finally reached the Indian Cemetery in Happy Valley. The funeral arrangement office had erected a shed in the square near the cemetery for the farewell ceremony. The shed was more than ten feet long and wide, with a hall in the middle, a reception area for guests on the left, and a chorus, Confucius, Zhengsheng, and silver bands on the right. Wu's portrait was hung in the center of the hall, surrounded by fresh flowers, with the horizontal inscription "Spirit Immortal" written by Tang Shaoyi above it, accompanied by a mourning couplet from Hu Hanmin. Both the couplet and the calligraphy were written by Hu himself in the style of Cao Quan. The text read, "The departed is like this, a loss for the party and the country; harmonious but not flowing, reminiscent of the ancient ministers." When the hearse arrived, the pallbearers placed the coffin in the hall. The coffin was Western-style and covered with the flag of the Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Wholly Red Earth. Then, the mourners paid their respects and dispersed.

After the relatives and friends bid farewell, at 5:00 PM, the coffin was taken to the crematorium by the children and relatives for cremation. First, the Indian minister prayed to the corpse, and then the corpse was moved out and put into the crematorium to be burned. At this time, Wu's wife and children wailed as if they would die. The relatives and friends present were also shedding tears. The corpse was burned for several hours, and by 7:00 PM, it had been turned to ashes. It is heard that Wu had determined that he wanted the same cremation ceremony that his father, Dr. Tingfang, had when he died. Therefore, his family's actions were in accordance with his wishes.

Anhui Implements Sales and Transportation of Huai Salt on a Rotation Basis 66

Salt Merchants Unwilling to Open Warehouses Due to Increased Tax Rates

Representatives from Taizhou and Suzhou Request the Ministry of Finance to Reduce Tax Rates

Anqing Correspondence: The transportation of edible salt to Anhui has traditionally been carried out through Datong. Recently, the Ministry of Finance approved the trial sale of 100 tickets of Huai Salt on a rotating basis in Anqing. Salt merchants organized the Continental Salt Company and established a general sales office at Taiyi Salt Shop on Tonganmen Main Street outside the West Gate of Anqing. It officially opened its warehouses on December 27 of last year. Officials from the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office of the Ministry of Finance were dispatched to weigh the salt in the warehouse and established the following regulations for selling salt: (1) Shore Price: 12.1 yuan per brand for counties with flat taxes, 13.1 yuan per brand for counties with heavy taxes in Taihu, Susong, Wangjiang, and Zhide, and 11.1 yuan per brand for Qianshan, a county with light taxes. (2) Weight per catty: According to the Transportation Bureau's weight standard, 100 catties per stone. (3) Tare weight: According to the regulations of the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office, each jute bag is deducted 3 catties and 12 taels for tare weight, and no ropes are allowed to be added. Recently, the Anqing Continental Salt Company received an order from the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office of the Ministry of Finance to implement the new system of weights and measures from January 1st of this year. Due to the increased tax rate, the company is unwilling to open for business. Yang Huicun and Chen Xuehang, representatives of the chambers of commerce in Taihu and Susong counties stationed in the province, argued that under the new system of weights and measures, each dan (unit of weight) is 15 catties less than the old system, but the tax rate remains the same. The supervisory effect has been reduced, but the tax has increased, effectively adding more than three yuan to each dan. Moreover, salt merchants from counties such as Taihu and Susong gather in the provincial capital, trade is stagnant, and there is a shortage of edible salt. Yesterday, a special telegram was sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting that the Salt Affairs Agency be ordered to instruct the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office to reduce taxes after the new weights and measures have been implemented in order to relieve the merchants and alleviate the people's difficulties. (January 6th)

Sichuan Mianzhu Massacre: Eight Members of a Family Poisoned to Death 67

The Culprits Were a Male Servant and the Mistress

They Fled Immediately After Committing the Crime and Disappeared

According to a Sichuan dispatch, a case was recently discovered in Mianzhu County, in which eight members of the Deng family were murdered by their wicked servant, Liu Zhengkui, and an adulterous woman, Wang. Liu and Wang immediately eloped. Deng Mingchen and other members of the Deng clan have offered a reward for their capture and prosecution. This case has significant implications for public morality and human conscience. The petition from Deng Mingchen and others is transcribed below:

"To all benevolent gentlemen of Sichuan Province, Deng Mingchen, Zhao Donglin, and others respectfully report: a case of poisoning an entire family, with grievances profound and unredressed. We offer a reward and earnestly request assistance in apprehending the culprits. Deng Zeyi, courtesy name Yizhi, is a native of Mianzhu County, residing in the Chicken Market Dam on the North Street of the town. His ancestors were wealthy in eastern Mianzhu, owning the Yiyuan Garden, commonly known as the Deng Family Garden. His great-grandfather, Changling, was a tribute student in the Guiyou year of the Jiaqing era, appointed as Prefect of Bao’an Prefecture in Zhili. His great-grandfather, Juchen, served as a prefectural clerk; his grandfather, Mingke, was a student of the county school; and his father, Dejun, was awaiting appointment as magistrate of Tongzhou. Zeyi was his son. After the Jiawu year of the Guangxu era, the family moved to the county town. His first wife, Li, bore no children; his birth mother, Zheng, remained a widow and managed the household for over twenty years. Zeyi's first wife, Zhao, was the second daughter of Donglin. She died young. He then remarried Yang, who raised a daughter but also passed away. He then remarried another Yang, who also died, leaving behind a son. Zeyi's marital fate was considered unfavorable, and he was said to bring misfortune to his wives, making it difficult to find a suitable match. He then went to Chengdu and bought Wang. At that time, the servant Liu Zhengkui attended to his daily needs. Liu had been with the family for eight or nine years. The master treated him well, and he was obedient. The household consisted of ten people: Zeyi, his mother and children, a six-year-old daughter, a three-year-old son, a hired wet nurse named Guo, a cook, another servant woman and her son, plus the servant Liu and Wang. During the previous Red Bandit unrest, Zeyi and his family remained behind closed doors, so relatives and friends rarely visited. This continued until October, when tenant farmers and local leaders came to collect rent and the investigation bureau came to collect money, repeatedly seeking Zeyi but unable to find him. They inquired with Donglin and others, who also had not heard from him for a long time. They then went to inquire with the caretaker of the house. The caretaker was an old woman with an unfamiliar face. According to her, she was hired by Liu Zhengkui on the eighth day of the eighth month to watch the house. When the two women arrived, they did not see Zeyi. Only Liu Zhengkui and Wang were there. Liu told her that the Zeyi family had gone to the provincial capital, but the young master's mother was still at home and would be leaving soon, instructing her to watch the house. The two women also said that Wang and Liu left together on the night of the eleventh day of the eighth month. Upon hearing the caretaker's words, Donglin and others were shocked. They immediately sent people to search for them in the provincial capital and neighboring counties, but to no avail. They searched all the relatives and friends in the county town, but they disappeared without a trace. Donglin then presented a petition to the local leader Dai Qingyun and relatives Zheng Yongquan, Hou Haibo, and others, reporting the situation to the county government. An investigation was ordered, and they went to the house with criminal investigators. The doors were unlocked, and the furniture was intact. They then opened the back door and went to a secluded area, where they found an area with no grass, covered with slag. They were greatly surprised. They ordered people to dig it up in front of everyone. First, they dug through ash, then charcoal ash, then bricks and stones, and then they saw a leg bone. Everyone was horrified and immediately reported it to the county government. The county magistrate, judicial officials, the city defense command, and the public security bureau all arrived in person. In front of everyone, they ordered people to dig up eight bodies of men, women, and children, all in one pit. They were all decomposed, with only white bones remaining. Seeing this tragic scene, everyone was filled with compassion and tears streamed down their faces. It was then discovered that Liu Zhengkui, in collusion with Wang, had plotted to kill the entire family of eight for their wealth and had secretly fled in the night. This wicked servant betrayed his master, and the adulterous woman killed her husband. What did the young children know? What was the fault of the laborers? They were all poisoned to death. This inhumanity has reached its extreme. The clan leader Deng Mingchen and relative Zhao Donglin have repeatedly petitioned the county government. County Magistrate Luo has dispatched a team to strictly arrest them and has offered a reward for information leading to their arrest, so they can be punished according to the law. We deeply fear that the wicked servant and the adulterous woman will flee far away, and people will not know their wicked deeds, allowing them to escape justice. Therefore, we are making this public announcement. Anyone who captures the adulterous woman Wang or the wicked servant Liu Zhengkui, the Deng family is willing to offer a reward of one thousand silver dollars. For the capture of either man or woman, a reward of six hundred silver dollars will be given. We earnestly request all gentlemen to pay attention to the investigation. If they can be apprehended, the reward money is currently held in Mianzhu, with Deng family members and Zhao Donglin responsible. We will not break our promise. We respectfully announce this to all people in Sichuan Province. If anyone obtains this notice, please widely circulate and post it in public places, so that everyone knows. If the true culprits are caught and the grievances are redressed, not only will we be grateful and never forget, but the wronged souls of the Deng family will also bow their heads in gratitude from the afterlife. We respectfully announce this and ask for your compassion. Deng Mingchen, Zhao Donglin, Zheng Yongquan, Hou Haibo, and others of Mianzhu County jointly present this."

Travel Notes on Sichuan and Xikang 68

— Lixing

｜From Shanghai to Nanjing｜ (1)

The Shanghai Journalists' Sichuan-Xikang Observation Group boarded the Minsheng Company's Yongnian steamer on the evening of the 6th to head west. The six members of the group are Gu Zhizhong, Zhang Xianmei, Chen Youqin, Lu Yi, Tang Huiping, and Wang Zhenhuan. The significance of this trip lies in the fact that since the Northeast has fallen, those who speak of observation must include the Northwest. However, people are largely unaware that Sichuan, Xikang, or some southwestern provinces, are simultaneously under the intense pressure of several imperialists. Their perilous situation and importance are nearly equal to those of the Northwest. Moreover, the Tibetan side has been incited and engaged in warfare year-round, already occupying areas east of central Xikang. The people of our country must not neglect this due to the remoteness of the location or the sudden rise of political conflicts in the Central Plains. We believe it is necessary to observe its current situation. Furthermore, in today's world, everyone is gathering their strength to seek a way out in the same direction. This is why the country has so many troubles. If those who harbor great ambitions prepare to sacrifice and endure hardship, starting with the most basic work, then the country's affairs would not have come to this. If news reporters also compete in the same direction, the information obtained will be too similar, bland, and rarely exciting. Moreover, before these political conflicts are resolved, even the most ordinary and inferior military and political news is subject to fragmentation and dismemberment. From the perspective of the news reporters themselves, in an environment where they are mentally suffering, it seems more appropriate to open up another path, seek another bright road, and obtain news with a completely different flavor.

That evening, the group members were too tired from packing, and they all fell sound asleep after going to bed. When they woke up at dawn, the Yongnian steamer had already moved westward. During breakfast on the 7th, the steamer's manager, Mr. Xie Sasheng, spoke enthusiastically about the scenery of Sichuan, particularly the clouds and rain of the Wu Mountains, inspiring their imagination. The food and drink on board were very comfortable. After a heavy fog that night, heavy snow followed. The steamer lost its direction and had to stop the engine and wait for the right time to move. It started again at 11 PM, but when they woke up in the morning, the fog returned, and the ship stopped moving again. It moved and stopped in this manner until 10:30 AM on the 8th, when they finally arrived in Nanjing.

The estimated itinerary is roughly ten days to reach Hankou, fourteen days to reach Yichang, twenty days to reach Chongqing, and twenty-three or twenty-four days to reach Chengdu. However, if there are changes in the weather, delays or postponements in the journey will be inevitable. (8th)

The Work of the Lunan Archaeological Team Concludes 69

The excavation of the Anshang Site has been completed

Over seventy boxes of artifacts are transported to Jinan for sorting

Jinan correspondence: The Lunan Archaeological Team, jointly formed by the Academia Sinica and the Shandong Antiquities Research Association, excavated the "Anshang Site" in Anshang Village, Teng County, and the Cao Wang Tomb in the three counties of Zou, Teng, and Yi in Lunan from October of last year. They searched for relics from the Spring and Autumn, Warring States, and Han periods to study China's ancient history, culture, and art. The excavation ended in early December. The people in charge of the excavation, Dong Zuobin, Qi Yanru, and others, arrived in Jinan one after another from Teng, stayed at the Antiquities Research Association, and sorted and studied the relics they brought with them. However, there are still over seventy boxes (matchbox size) of collected relics, such as pottery shards, bones, and painted stones, stored in the home of Mr. Huang Futang, a local elder in Teng County. Due to the failure to negotiate the transportation properly, they have not been fully transported to Jinan. The Academia Sinica has notified the Jinpu Railway Bureau to approve the loading and transportation to Jinan. Dong Zuobin has already gone to Anyang, Henan, to inspect the local excavation of antiquities, and is not in Jinan. Wang Xiang and Qi Yanru boarded the first Jinpu train at 9:30 AM today (the 6th) to go to Teng for transportation. They should be able to return to Jinan within a few days. It is reported that Wang and others have recently completed the restoration of broken pieces of dou (stemmed bowl), li (tripod cauldron), and fou (jar) unearthed at the Anshang Village and Cao Wang Tomb, closely resembling the original objects. In addition, the Shandong Provincial Library recently purchased a pair of stone Han sheep for 250 yuan, said to be unearthed in Shou County, Anhui Province. After verification by Wang Xiantang and others, they are confirmed to be Han Dynasty relics, sacrificial images displayed in front of the tomb passage. There are about eight or nine characters on each sheep, but they are difficult to identify at this time due to corrosion. They are currently being cleaned, and it is expected that they will make contributions to the study of Han Dynasty history and culture in the future. (6th)

Songjiang Water Police Rescue Kidnapped Victim from Danger 70

Fan Guozhong, the captain of the third squadron of the water police, personally supervised Hu Tu, the leader of the second detachment, to lead investigators to rescue a kidnapped victim, Jiang Xingbo, from Qingpu Gaolu, at the home of Ding Afa east of Zhangjiatang on the border of Fengxian and Nanhui. The kidnappers, including Jin Amei, were taken into custody. During the preliminary interrogation, the kidnappers implicated several others. Captain Fan went to Shanghai that night and rescued a three-year-old Dai child from the home of Xu Chen in the Xiaoshadu area of Shanghai. The female bandit Xu Chen and her daughter Jin Nv were arrested on the spot. At the same time, Inspector Gu Lansheng was secretly dispatched to the Shihudang train station, where he arrested the main bandits in the kidnapping case of Jiang Xingbo and the Dai child, Xu Ade, Ding Afa, and Gu Yunlong. Two pistols and thirty-eight bullets were found on Xu Ade and Ding Afa. It is learned that they have been handed over to the Minhang District Department for investigation.

County Chamber of Commerce Elects Chairman 71

The executive and supervisory committee members of the County Chamber of Commerce were re-elected at the end of last month. Today (the 8th) was the day for the executive and supervisory committee members to take office and elect five standing committee members. The county magistrate, Jin Tigan, party secretary Sun Shiheng, and leaders of various agencies attended the meeting. Cai Zhongyu, Yang Zhimin, Yang Yunsheng, Cheng Weiru, and Zhu Yian were elected as standing committee members, and Cai Zhongyu was elected as chairman. Cai initially declined the position in public, but after repeated persuasion by the committee members, he reluctantly agreed to accept it. He then stated that the chamber's affairs and documents must be jointly responsible by the standing committee members, to which everyone nodded in agreement and dispersed.

Caretaker of Chunyang Temple Robbed 72

The Chunyang Temple outside the South Gate of the Huangpu Bund has no property or incense offerings. Therefore, there are no monks, Taoists, or lay practitioners. Only the caretaker, Ayou, remains to watch the temple, grow vegetables, and raise chickens and ducks to make a living. His poverty is well known. However, six or seven robbers suddenly came the night before, dug a hole in the wall, struck Ayou on the back with an iron ruler, knocked him to the ground, and tied him up. They then entered the room, tied up two relatives of Ayou who were staying overnight, searched for clothes, chickens, and ducks, and fled. The three were tied up and unable to untie themselves until yesterday morning when villagers passing by heard their cries and came in to rescue them. It is truly strange that such a barren temple was also coveted by robbers.

Dispute Over Changing Scales for Salt in Wuxi 73

The salt sold by the local salt merchant guild has always been measured using the canal scale. The salt stores then resell it to retail customers using the salt scale, from which they can earn a small profit. Recently, all industries have switched to new scales. The salt guild has also followed suit. However, the new scale is smaller than the canal scale, and the wholesale price should also be reduced accordingly. However, the salt guild not only did not reduce the wholesale price but also canceled the old practice of deducting for rope. Therefore, the salt stores have no profit to make and strongly oppose it. They have repeatedly negotiated with the salt guild but have not achieved satisfactory results. Until yesterday, the salt guild agreed to consult with the Shanghai Salt Merchants Association before responding. It is unknown whether this will resolve the issue.

First Snow Brings Joy to Farmers 74

In recent months, there has been little rain or snow in the area, resulting in extreme drought. Fires have been frequent, and many residents are suffering from epidemics. Recently, the weather has been alternating between cold and warm. Yesterday (the 7th) afternoon at 4:00 PM, snow began to fall, becoming heavier at 7:00 PM and stopping at midnight, with an accumulation of about an inch. Farmers are all overjoyed.

Changzhou Physical Education Inspector Visits Changzhou 75

Pei Xiyuan, a special commissioner from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, was commissioned to inspect physical education in the five counties of Wujin, Yixing, Liyang, Jiangyin, and Jingjiang. Commissioner Pei has inspected the four counties of Yi, Li, Jing, and Cheng and arrived in Changzhou on the 7th. He inspected the county's sports field and inquired in detail. On the 8th, he visited Yang Haoming, the director of the Bureau of Education, to investigate the general situation of the funding for various agricultural education centers and sports fields. It is said that among the five counties, Yixing has the best physical education program, followed by Wujin, then Jiangyin and Jingjiang, with Liyang being the worst. Commissioner Pei completed his inspection of the counties and returned to Zhenjiang on the afternoon of the 8th to report his findings.

The Zhenjiang Shen Qingchen Case Concludes Debate 76

The case of Shen Qingchen, the former magistrate of Fengxian County, who was accused of corruption, involved Yang Changyou, the secretary who was accused of fraudulent acquisition of wealth, Xu Yongjiang, the chief of the fourth self-government district, Feng Wenchuan, the assistant, and Diao Yebai, a Chinese medicine practitioner in the county. They were transferred by the provincial government to the local court for investigation last year. Except for Shen Qingchen, who was dismissed by the prosecutor's office, Yang Changyou, Xu Yongjiang, and others were publicly prosecuted for taking advantage of their positions to intimidate and defraud others and transferred to the criminal court. Presiding Judge Zhou Baochu held several court hearings. Yesterday was the date for the debate. First, Tao Rong, the defense lawyer for Yang, stood up and argued that the defendant in this case was prosecuted for taking advantage of his position to intimidate and defraud others. The defendant was ordered by the county magistrate on March 20 last year to investigate whether Zhu Jinwen had communicated with the enemy. At that time, District Chief Xu Yongjiang and others were present during the conversation, and there was no opportunity for fraud. Moreover, the plaintiff Zhu Jinwen's statements were inconsistent. The defendant's statement in the Civil Affairs Department was made under duress at the time. Therefore, he should be thoroughly investigated and declared innocent. Then, Chen Liren, the defense lawyer for Feng Wenchuan, and Fang Enpu, the defense lawyer for Diao Yebai, gave their arguments. Judge Zhou then declared the debate closed. The defendants Yang Changyou and Xu Yongjiang were remanded in custody, Diao Yebai was released on the original bail, and Feng Wenchuan was required to provide an additional 400 yuan in written bail. Tao Rong had requested bail for Yang Changyou, but it was not granted.

Small Steamers in Zhenjiang Join Forces 77

Since July of the 21st year, the small steamer industry on the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu route was united through an agreement among nine companies, operating on a daily rotation basis. Later, the Dada Company joined the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu route. The route was temporarily suspended due to low water levels in the canal. The long-distance Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu route was restored in April last year, but the long-distance traffic was disrupted again due to floods and fires. After the floodwaters receded, Dada Company requested to join the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu route and operate the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu service, based on the order of the Ministry of Communications. In order to maintain the status quo, the nine companies agreed to Dada's request. At the same time, Jiangtai Company also requested the same treatment as Dada. The Zhenjiang Shipping Industry Association believed that the Zhenjiang shipping industry was under environmental pressure and could not handle it. Therefore, it initiated a preparatory meeting for a large-scale joint operation of the upper and lower river shipping industries. However, although Jiangtai Company participated in the joint operation, it still insisted on opening the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu service first, as a precursor to gaining a foothold. At this point, the joint operation was once again obstructed. After discussions among various parties, it was finally decided that the Zhenjiang-Qingjiangpu service would be divided into 32 days per month. In addition to the nine companies, Dada Company would join and operate for two days per month. Dada would give four-tenths of its profits to Jiangtai. At the same time, preparations for the joint operation continued. The disputes on the Zhenjiang route were resolved at this point.

Nantong Prevents Banditry 78

The Seventh District Administrative Inspector's Office received reports that some people were taking advantage of banditry in the coastal areas of the district, intending to seize weapons and ammunition from the Bao Wei Tuan (local security force). Commissioner Cheng ordered all counties to strictly prevent this and ordered special nighttime vigilance in all villages and towns. The police teams of the five counties are implementing patrols.

Tongcheng Sees Its First Snow 79

The weather in Tongcheng was cold and overcast on the 7th. At 5:00 PM in the evening, snow began to fall, continuing until midnight.

Gaoyou Hall Commissioner 80

Shi Xingrui, the captain of the second detachment of the Gaoyou County Police Team, and Pian Futong, the acting captain of the fourth detachment, were previously ordered to suppress bandits in the tenth district. When they arrived in the district, because it was late, they requested Xia Meikui, the head of the tenth district Tuan Lian, to notify the Bao Wei Tuan in each township to avoid misunderstandings. However, when the two captains Shi and Pian passed through Zhujiadui, the Bao Wei Tuan there, suspecting them of being bandits, opened fire, wounding two soldiers of the second detachment, Zhou Dezong and Zhao Yufa. After Shi and Pian negotiated with the Bao Wei Tuan, they learned that District Head Xia had not notified them, causing the accident. They then questioned District Head Xia. After mediation by local people, District Head Xia and the Bao Wei Tuan each provided 30 yuan for medical expenses, which the injured soldiers used to go to the Datong Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, District Head Xia recently accused Police Captain Zhu Hua and the two captains Shi and Pian of extortion of 30 yuan to the Civil Affairs Department and the Ninth District Administrative Commissioner's Office. Dong Guangfu was appointed by the Civil Affairs Department to conduct a thorough investigation of this case together with Commissioner Ma Zhenbang. Commissioner Dong came to Gaoyou last night and investigated the case at the county government this morning. County Magistrate Yang reported the details of the incident to the provincial commission based on the police team's report. The provincial commissioner then ordered County Magistrate Yang to order the police to summon the plaintiff and witnesses for interrogation and submit them to the provincial commission for verification.

Hangzhou Arrests Thief Who Snatched Large Sum of Money from Bank 81

Yesterday (the 8th) morning at 11:00 AM, the Hangzhou branch of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank ordered Huang Xirong from Xiaoshan, a staff member, to take a matured check of more than 2,860 yuan issued by the local bank to exchange for cash. Huang took the check to exchange it, and the local bank paid Huang the full amount. Huang counted the money on the counter. After counting a thousand yuan, a middle-aged man wearing a gray silk robe and black mandarin jacket suddenly came forward, snatched the thousand-yuan bills counted by Huang, and fled into the crowd. Huang shouted for a thief and was caught by Lin Yuehua, a police officer hired by the bank. He was detained in the Public Security Bureau. According to his confession, he is from Shaoxing, named Zhou Afa, and runs a drugstore. He has an elderly mother, wife, and daughter at home. Because the Lunar New Year is approaching, he committed this act. He requested lenient treatment.

Female Teacher Commits Suicide Out of Shame 82

Lu Xiangwen, a woman from Henan, is 20 years old and quite beautiful. After graduating from the Henan Women's Normal School, she worked as a village school teacher. Because she was young and liked to travel, she was seduced and lost her virginity by a man from Anhui named Hua. Her father found out about it and scolded her slightly. Therefore, Xiangwen had no face to stay at home. She came to Hangzhou last month and stayed at her classmate Wang's home at the foot of Geling Mountain in West Lake, intending to find a job and make a living. Unexpectedly, after several days, there was no hope. Therefore, she had the idea of committing suicide, bought sleeping pills and swallowed them. Fortunately, her classmate noticed and questioned her closely, and she confessed the truth. She was immediately rescued and did not lose her life. Wang asked someone to accompany her back to her hometown in Henan yesterday (the 8th) morning.

Sun Ke Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Spoke 83

Said Hu Hanmin Indicated He Has No Intention of Going to Nanjing for Now

The Southwest's Understanding of the Central Government Has Increased

Hu's Stance is Against the Matter, Not Against the Person

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, traveled to the Philippines with his wife and others at the end of the year for a sea voyage. He made a stop in Hong Kong and Guangdong, where he visited Hu Hanmin, Chen Jitang, and other Central Committee members in the Southwest to discuss the current situation. He arrived in Shanghai on the Gran Tronto ship of the Da Lai Company at 8:30 yesterday morning, accompanied by Chuan Bingchang and others. His wife plans to stay in Guangdong for a few days and did not come with him. After arriving in Shanghai, Sun told reporters that Hu Zhantang has no intention of coming to Nanjing, and the rumors of a third government in Guangdong are completely unfounded. The details are recorded as follows:

Arrival Situation The Da Lai Company's Gran Tronto ship entered the port at 7:30 yesterday morning and docked at the Da Lai Wharf in Bailianjing, Pudong. Legislative Yuan members Ma Chaojun, Chen Jianru, Wu Jingxiong, Secretary-General Liang Hancao, Vice Minister of Industry Liu Weizhi, Vice Minister of Interior Chuan Rulin, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Yu Ming, Director of the Municipal Security Department Yang Hu, Chief of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Wu Xingya, and Secretary of the Municipal Government Tang Shixuan all boarded the ship to welcome him. At 8:30, Sun landed at the Jianghai Customs Wharf and went directly to his private residence on Columbia Road to rest. He plans to stay in Shanghai for one or two days before returning to Nanjing to report the details of his trip to the Central Government.

Accompanying Personnel Those who came with Sun yesterday were Legislative Yuan member Chuan Bingchang, Secretary Yang Huayi, and attendants. The wife of former Aviation Director Zhang Huichang also came to Shanghai on the same ship. As for Mrs. Sun, Chen Shuying, she did not come with him because her two sons are studying at Lingnan University in Guangzhou.

Sun's Talk After returning to his residence, Sun immediately received reporters from various newspapers. According to him, he went to Hong Kong with his wife for a sea trip and visited Hu Zhantang. Then he went to Guangdong and met with Xiao Focheng, Chen Bonan, and others to exchange views on the current situation. As a result, he plans to submit Hu's eight proposals, published in Hong Kong on December 17 last year, to the Central Standing Committee for discussion first, to see what everyone thinks, and then make a decision on whether to submit them as a proposal to the Fourth Central Committee, which will also be decided after discussion at the meeting.

Southwest Attitude Sun also said that he only stayed in Guangzhou for one day, so he did not have much time to discuss the details with the Southwest Committee. He only met with Chen Bonan and others to discuss matters. He learned that the Guangdong Committee generally agreed with Hu's proposals on political issues. As for what method to use to accept his proposals in the future, it was not discussed. Of the eight principles advocated by Hu, only four are more important: (1) The military must not interfere in politics, and military power belongs to the government; (2) Civil rights must be liberated, and the people's freedom of speech, publication, assembly, and association must be effectively protected; (3) The central government and the provinces implement equal rights and their methods; (4) Finance is open, and the budget system is implemented. Hu has no intention of coming to Nanjing for now. As for the issue of people, Hu did not talk about it at all. In short, the result of this trip to the South by Central Committee member Zhang Puquan and others has increased the Southwest's understanding of the Central Government.

Hu and Others on Fujian Sun also said that Hu and other Central Committee members in the Southwest strongly disapprove of the absurd actions of Chen Mingshu and others in Fujian this time, destroying the party and the country. Therefore, they deeply hope that Chen and others can repent as soon as possible and voluntarily abolish the so-called "People's Government." As for whether the Central Government will temporarily end the military after occupying Fuzhou and use political means to solve other problems, he is still not sure because he is traveling. In short, besides using military means to sanction the Fujian incident, there is no other proper way. He plans to stay in Shanghai for a few days before returning to Beijing.
